Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 393
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
景
Scenery
E
The Scenery Door 景門
Introduction
The Scenery Door is a Liaison Officer. Its origins are from the Li Palace
of the South, and it belongs to Fire. Li represents Fire, South, Summer
and middle maiden. The weather and temperature in the South is warm
and the scenery is beautiful during the Summer.
As Li represents daughter, it counters Qian Metal (father) and clashes
with Kan Water (husband). Therefore, it shows that the relationship will
be harmonious, close and loving. But disharmony will bring disaster and
even calamity as well. Hence, this is called the Scenery Door.
When Scenery Door resides in its home Palace of Li, it is called “Fu
Yin 伏吟". If it resides in Kun Palace 1, it is called “Fan Yin 反吟". When
Scenery Door is in the Qian Palace 6, it is called Entering Graveyard 入
墓, and if it is in the Dui Palace 7, it becomes Compelled. In Palaces of
Zhen 3 and Xun, it is Greater Auspicious and when it is in the Palaces
of Kun 2 and Gen 3, it is Lesser Auspicious.

only favorable for matters related to documentation and paperwork. As
such, it is suitable for submitting a written document to a high authority,
presenting a statement or selecting troops for battle. Other things,
however, remain unfavorable. It is auspicious in Palaces of Kun, Gen and
Center; stable in Zhen Palace 3 and Xun Palace 4, Fan Yin in Kan Palace
1, and Compelling in Qian Palace 6. It is inauspicious in Dui Palace 7.

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 409
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
死
Death
E
The Death Door 死門
Introduction
The Death Door originates from the Southwest, where Kun resides. This
door governs punishment, killing and hidden matters. It belongs to the
Earth Element. Kun represents mother, warehouse, winter, convergence,
darkness, concealment and death.
As with everything on Earth, there is a beginning as well as an end.
There must be a home to return to even after death. This is why it is
called the Death Door, to mark the end of a journey.
When Death Door resides in its home Palace of Kun 2, it is called “Fu
Yin 伏吟". If it resides in Gen Palace 8, it is called “Fan Yin 反吟". When
Death Door is in the Xun Palace 4, it is called Entering Graveyard 入
墓, and if it is in the Zhen Palace 3, it becomes Countered 受制. In the
Li Palace 9, it is represented as Greater Inauspicious with Producing
Prosperity and when it is in the Kan Palace 1, it is Greater Inauspicious.
It is Compelled and inter-producing when it is in the Palaces of Qian 6
and Dui 7.

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 425
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
驚
Fear
E
The Fear Door 驚門
Introduction
The Fear Door governs suprise and damage. It originates from the
West where the Dui Palace resides, and belongs to Metal element. Dui
represents lake, autumn, shortage, metal, young women, shock, pain,
quarrel, lawsuit, fear and anger.
In the season of autumn, cold air chills the atmosphere and plants are
close to wither. After the peak of summer, mother nature’s energy is
slows down; atmosphere is gloomy and cold, quarrels are aplenty. It’s
difficult to avoid disagreements and discontentment. As fear, worries
and all other mixed emotions are abound at this period, this is why it is
called the Fear Door.
When Fear Door resides in its home Palace of Dui 7, it is called “Fu Yin
伏吟". If it resides in Zhen Palace 3, it is called “Fan Yin 反吟". When Fear
Door is in the Gen Palace 8, it is called Entering Graveyard 入墓, and if
it is in the Li Palace 9, it becomes Countered 受制. In the Xun Palace
4, it is Compelled and when it is in the Kan Palace 1, it is Discouraged.
Fear Door in the Kun Palace 2 is inter-producing, and while in the Qian
Palace 6, it is Harmony.

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 441
奇

遁

鑑
F
The 9 Stars 九星
There are three factors that govern the success or failure of an event:
Right Place, Right Time, Right People. In Chinese Metaphysics this is
known as the principle of Heaven, Earth, Man.
The 9 Stars in Qi Men Dun Jia represent the Heavenly Matters 天時.
This means they symbolize the “Right Time” aspect of events and
circumstances. The 9 Stars also represent the movement of the heavenly
or celestial bodies (Stars) and their impact on earth and humans.
The 9 Stars are established based on the 9 Palaces and the 8 Trigrams
of the Luo Shu. They are believed to be a reference to the Big Dipper 北
斗星 stream of stars. The 9 Stars in Qi Men are the Heavenly Grass 天蓬
星 (Water), the Heavenly Grain 天芮星 (Earth), the Heavenly Destructor
天沖星 (Wood), the Heavenly Assistant 天輔星 (Wood), the Heavenly
Bird 天禽星 (Earth), the Heavenly Heart 天心星 (Metal), the Heavenly
Pillar 天柱星 (Metal), the Heavenly Ambassador 天任星 (Earth) and the
Heavenly Hero 天英星 (Fire).
九星
The 9 Stars
北斗七星
North Dipper 9 Star
天蓬星 The Heavenly Grass 	貪狼星 Greedy Wolf
天芮星 The Heavenly Grain 	巨門星 Huge Door
天沖星 The Heavenly Destructor 	祿存星 Fortune Treasures
天輔星 The Heavenly Assistant 	文曲星 Literary Arts
天禽星 The Heavenly Bird 	廉貞星 Chastity
天心星 The Heavenly Heart 	武曲星 Military Arts
天柱星 The Heavenly Pillar 	破軍星 Broken Soldier

天英星 The Heavenly Hero 	右弼星 Right Assistant

-- 453 of 810 --

442 Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
F
The Heavenly Matters 天時 or “Timing” – include not only the influence
of space and Mother Nature (然界的天時氣象), it also include the
laws of the society and social development, including the political
climate, economic conditions, market conditions and social welfare.
To a particular person, the Heavenly Matters also represent one’s
genetic factors, innate quality, personality, cultural background and
fundamental nature.
Each of the 9 Stars corresponds to one of the sectors in the Luo Shu as
its original home palace: the palace of Kan 坎 1 for instance, corresponds
to the Heavenly Grass 天蓬星, the palace of Kun 坤 2 corresponds to
the Heavenly Grain 天芮星, the palace of Zhen 震 3 corresponds to
the Heavenly Destructor 天沖星, the palace of Xun 巽 4 corresponds
to the Heavenly Assistant 天輔星, the Middle 5 palace corresponds
to the Heavenly Bird 天禽星, the palace of Qian 乾 6 corresponds to
the Heavenly Heart 天心星, the palace of Dui 兌 7 corresponds to the
Heavenly Pillar 天柱星, the palace of Gen 艮 8 corresponds to the
Heavenly Ambassador 天任星 and the palace of Li 離 9 corresponds to
the Heavenly Hero 天英星.
九星

The 9 Stars are arranged in this sequence: the Heavenly Grass 天蓬
星, the Heavenly Grain 天芮星, the Heavenly Destructor 天沖星, the
Heavenly Assistant 天輔星, the Heavenly Bird 天禽星, the Heavenly
Heart 天心星, the Heavenly Pillar 天柱星, the Heavenly Ambassador 天
任星 and the Heavenly Hero 天英星. There are nine Yang Dun Ju 陽遁
and nine Yin Dun Ju 陰遁 in Qi Men, but regardless of the Yang Dun or
the Yin Dun, the 9 Stars are always arranged in a clockwise sequence.

九星
The 9 Stars
解說
Description
天
蓬
星
The Heavenly
Grass Star
This star is of the Water element and it corresponds to
the Kan 坎 Trigram. It’s a Yang polarity star in Qi Men.
This star indicates theft, looting and tyranny; as such,
it is generally regarded as an inauspicious star. It is not
good for marriage, long-distance travel, construction
and development. But it is usable for making money
or operating a business when it is accompanied by
the Yi Noble 日奇, the Bing Noble 月奇 and the Life
Door 生門.
天
芮
星
The Heavenly
Grain
This star is of the Earth element and a Yin polarity
star in Qi Men. It represents sickness. In divination, it
symbolizes disease, decay and darkness and generally
regarded as an inauspicious star. Since it epitomizes
darkness, the common advice when this star is
received should be to advocate morality and pursue
proper teachings and education. This personifies the
act of receiving ‘light’ to the darkness.
天
沖
星
The Heavenly
Destructor
As the Wood element and a Yang polarity star, the
Heavenly Destructor corresponds to the East of Zhen
震 Palace (3). It represents sudden activity, action,
shake-up, moving and executing. It is full of vibrant
energy. It’s a moderately auspicious star in Qi Men.

柱

is considered an immovable star with strong, fierce
will. It relates to damages and pain. This is why it is
regarded as an inauspicious star.

The 9 Palaces Corresponding to the 9 Heavenly Star Map
The natal (or original) corresponding sectors of the 9 Stars with the
8 Trigrams are fixed. For convenience, practitioners may remove the
phrase “Heavenly” from their names. In the Qi Men plate, the 9 Stars
represent heavenly events or matters and thus, they are often considered
as the Heavenly Plate. By referring to the Leader of the Heavenly Stems,
we could determine the location of both the Lead Star and the Envoy.
The purpose is to arrange the 9 Stars into the Qi Men chart.
The Strengths of the 9 Stars
The strengths of the 9 Stars are determined by the timing in which the
reading is done. The timing is based on the Chinese solar calendar.

The 9 Stars will exert different qualities in different periods of the year.
Each star has positive and negative attributes. How influential are
they in a Qi Men reading depends greatly on whether they are at the
Prosperous 旺 , Strong 相, Useless 廢, Trapped 囚 or Weak 休 stages.

-- 462 of 810 --

F
Are the Strengths for the 9 Stars only influenced by the
Seasons? Or are they influenced by other parties in the
Qi Men chart?
In Qi Men, the Prosperous, Strong, Useless, Trapped or Weak stages
are determined by the season of the reading. The season dictates the
degree of influence the 9 Stars would have on the environment around
them. More specifically, this means the influence that the 9 Stars would
have on the 8 Doors and the Stems in the Qi Men chart in different
months of the year.
For instance, the Fire of Bing 丙 and Ding 丁 is timely in the beginning
and middle of the summer months. When they meet with the Heavenly
Destructor 天沖星 and the Heavenly Assistant Stars 天輔星 (which belong
to the Wood element), the Wood of these two stars will encourage the
Fire to burn, hence achieving even more brightness and strength. This is
called the Strong相 stage.
However, when these two stems meet with the Heavenly Hero Star 天英
星, which belongs to the Fire, they can only be considered in the Strong
stage because the Fire is originally in the timely status, and the Heavenly
Hero Star is merely adding into this stage.
When the Bing and Ding of Fire meet with the Heavenly Ambassador 天
任星 and the Heavenly Grain of the Earth element, the Earth can’t play a
role in this equation, so it’s considered to be in the Useless 廢 stage.
When these two stems meet with the Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 of the
Water element, the Fire (being in the summer) would be in a timely
stage, although the Water could control the Fire. In another words, the
Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 is considered to be in the Weak休 stage.
When the two Fire Stems meet with the Heavenly Pillar and the Heavenly
Heart Star of the Metal element, these two Stars will be Trapped囚 as it
is timely for the Fire of Bing and Ding in the summer.

The Nine Stars and the Eight Doors Matching with the
Trigrams Method
1. 	The Heavenly Grass 天蓬星, the Heavenly
Ambassador, 天任星 the Heavenly Assistant 天輔星,
and the Heavenly Bird 天禽星 are the Yang Stars.
2. 	The Heavenly Hero 天英星, the Heavenly Grain 天芮星,
the Heavenly Pillar 天柱星, and the Heavenly Heart 天
心星 are the Yin Stars.
3. 	The Heavenly Assistant 天輔星, the Heavenly Bird
天禽星 and the Heavenly Heart 天心星 are highly
auspicious. The Heavenly Destructor and the Heavenly
Ambassador 天任星 are rarely auspicious.
4. 	The Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 and the Heavenly Grain 天
芮星 are highly inauspicious. The Heavenly Hero 天
英星 and the Heavenly Pillar 天柱星 are moderately
inauspicious.
The Envoy, which is the Lead Door, needs to be matched with the Lead
Star, which is one of the 9 Stars. When a Trigram is shown with the
location of the Envoy, it is recognized as the Internal Gua. In contrast,
the location of the Lead Star is called the External Gua Trigram. We can
call these two locations in Qi Men as the Original Life Gua 本命卦.

F
The Host and the Guest Judgment in the 9 Stars
The Basic Concept
In Qi Men we can classify the 9 Stars of the Heavenly Plate as the Guest
客, and the 9 Stars of the Earth Plate as the Host 主.
It is important to distinguish between the Host and Guest in a Qi
Men analysis. This principle of object and subject is prevalent in
throughout the entire practice of Qi Men. For instance, in a battle,
will you actively assault or will you exhaust your enemy and wait for
the right time to strike? Will you consider an open attack or a sneak
attack in a business dealing?
主
Host
The quiet one, always passive; it is a defender, favors
proximity, and internal environment.
客
Guest
Is always moving and takes initiative; the attacker,
favors distance, and external environment.
The Judgment Method of Host and Guest of the 9 Stars
There are advantages and disadvantages for each the Guest and the
Host in the 9 Stars analysis in Qi Men. Even though a basic reading of
a star can be “negative,” the situation can be reversed if and when we
change our position from the Host to the Guest or from the Guest to the
Host.

-- 466 of 810 --

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 455
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
F
The Basic Principles
When two of the same elements reside in the same Heaven or Earth
Plate of the 9 Stars, it’s called the Bi He 比和, which denotes harmony.
For instance, the Bi He 比和 can be found when Metal element resides
with Metal or when Fire resides with Fire element in a particular palace.
It is very advantageous for both the Host and the Guest to meet in
palaces that are in the Produce and the Prosperous stage. This indicates
a positive outcome in everything you do and victory will likely grace the
outcome of your battle.
If the location of discourse is in the Grave 墓 or the Weakening 衰 stage,
it is recommended that you delay your important endeavors. This makes
it advantageous for the Host. Where the timing is not ripe, it is better to
plan an ambush or a hidden scheme.
If the location is at the Death 死絕 stage, it can turn to the Day Stem
for help. This is called the Rescue from Desperation 絕處逢生. In this
situation, it is advantageous for the Host 利主 as it is favors the party
that acts later.
It is disadvantageous however, to be either the Host or Guest when the
timing is Dead 死 and is controlled by the Day and the Hour Stem. In this
situation, the Qi is lacking and it is already at a futile stage. Both the Host
and the Guest will not succeed.
As long as the 9 Stars are in the Prosperous or the Strong 旺相
stage, “timely”, they are not afraid of being Clashed 沖、Countered
剋、Restrained 制、or Harmed 害. The end result is always positive.
If the 9 Stars are at the Prosperous or the Strong stage and meet with
further enhancement or support from other elements – it is known as
the Prosperity above Prosperity 喜上加喜. In other words, it is a highly
favorable condition.

-- 467 of 810 --

456 Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
F
In contrast, when the stars are in the Dead, the Useless or the Trapped
stages, the situation would worsen when they meet with the Clashed
沖、the Countered 剋、the Restrained 制、or the Harmed 害.
There is a difference in assuming either the role of the Host or the Guest
in any situation. Certain circumstances favor the Host, while others favor
the Guest.
Being the Host, there are certain rules or formality to follow. For instance,
the Host is usually guided by the principle of Gratitude and Growth 施
恩報德 選將求賢, which revolves around performing good deeds to win
others and advancing ahead in goals and career.
Hence the good Host, in order to gain traction in his or her desire or
goals, will embark on activities that could lead to an outflow of cash.
And if everything should go in accordance to strategy, there would be an
initial outflow of resources and this needs to be measured and controlled
carefully to avoid serious losses.
For instance, when the Host meets with the Water based subjects like
the Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 Star, the Rest Door 休門, Ren壬 Water Stem
or Gui 癸 Water Stem, the Host will likely treat his or her guests to a
fine dining experience, party by the lake or enjoy a luxurious cruise ride
down the river. But if there are also ‘negative’ formations in the chart, this
indicates a (Water element) false alarm or a water-based illness.
Whether a situation is beneficial to the Host or the Guest depends on
the relationship between the Heaven Plate 9 Stars and the original, natal
Earth Plate Nine Stars.
Where the Heaven Plate 9 Stars are countering the Earth Plate 9 Stars, the
Guest is more advantageous. And if the Earth Plate 9 Stars is countering
the Heaven Plate 9 Stars, then it would be more advantageous for the
Host.

The Judgment in Specific Circumstances
Guest Harming the Host
When the Heavenly Plate 9 Stars is countering the Earthly Plate 9 Stars,
we call this the “Guest Harming the Host”. In such a situation, it is more
advantageous to be the Guest.
To be the Guest means to be proactive. This means in war, one must be
the first to take offence, as the one who strikes first gains upper hand in
the situation. This is what it means to be the Guest.
This arrangement is disadvantageous to the Host. The Host is usually
the passive one in the given situation. Hence it is disadvantageous if
you plan to just hold meetings to discuss strategy, undertaking Public
Relations activities or performing good deeds or attending conference.
When the Heavenly Plate 9 Stars is at the Prosperous stage and the
Earthly Plate 9 Stars is at the Weakening stage, the situation would turn
out inauspicious for the Host.
Being the Host means being inactive or being responsive instead of
proactive. Hence opt for activeness in whatever you do as you’re likely
to obtain positive results for activities such as strategy execution and
offensive first-on approach.
The Heavenly Plate cannot harm the Earthly Plate when its location of
discourse is at the Death and when it is at the Weakening stage. When
the Wood is in the Prosperous stage, however, it is auspicious to assume
the role of the Host. But the Host would succumb to diseases when the
Earthly Plate is in the Weakening and the Death stage.

Guest Produces The Host
When the Heavenly Plate of the 9 Stars produces the Earthly Plate of the
9 Stars, this arrangement is called the “Guest produces the Host.” Such
situation would be advantageous for the Host. As they favor passivity
and inactiveness in their actions, they would thrive on matters such as
planning and strategizing.
If the Heavenly Plate resides in the Weakening Stage, while the Earthly
Plate is in the Prosperous stage, it is called the “Weak Wood Producing
Fire.” The situation would end up beneficial for the Host party, especially
in battle or dispute. If hidden moves or strategies are adopted, the
outcome would be more auspicious.
Guest Countering the Timely Host
When the Heavenly Plate of the 9 Stars counters the Earthly Plate that is in
the timely stage, we call it as the “Guest Countering the Timely Host.”
In the Prosperous stage, the Heavenly Plate could produce the Earthly
Plate, but the result would be insignificant. When it is in the Prosperous
stage, the Heavenly Plate denotes hidden attack in business and losing
out in a competition.
Host Harming The Guest
The Heavenly Plate 9 Stars is harming the Earthly Plate 9 Stars and as
such, this is what we refer to as the “Host Harming the Guest.”
Being the Host would be auspicious as he or she would attain success
for matters such as traveling, attaining fame or assuming managerial
position. But the Host should deter from any planning or strategizing
activities, as their execution will most likely to be flawed and inflict
exorbitant cost.

Host Producing the Guest
When the Earthly Plate of the 9 Stars produces the Heavenly Plate of the

The situation would be advantageous if you assume the role of the Guest.
It is beneficial for carrying out attacks that showcase your splendor
strengths and plan sound strategy that enable you to attain admirable
outcome. However, the Guest would need to contribute their fair share
of efforts and resources.

The 9 Star Evidence Occurrences 九星剋應
In Qi Men, particularly under the system called Fa Qi Men 法奇門,
practitioners learn to observe “evidence” from the living environment after
a specific 9 Star is applied or used to confirm if the special formation is
active and to ascertain if the predicted outcome would indeed become
a reality.
This technique is called the ‘Evidence Occurrence 外應' where the
practitioner will look for indicators as spelled out in the ancient classics.
Now, I’ve taken the liberty to include and translate all these indicators
here in the following sections of EACH of the 9 Star. They will be listed
under the topics:
1) 	Star with Hour Evidence Occurrences
2) 	Star with Door and Gua Evidence Occurrences
This section describes the occurrence of “evidence” you will see in your
living environment that tells you the special formations are activated.
As these sections are transliterated from ancient texts, some of the
descriptions may not at first make sense to you, or may even sound
weird or illogical. But bear in mind that these original texts were written
in ancient times and much of what they saw in their environment back
then is no longer the applicable today.
While the environment and culture have changed, the context or the
principle remains the same. What we need to do is to take the idea or
the concept and apply it to the modern setting.
I am tempted to translate and convert all the information here into my
view of how they are in the modern world, but have chosen not to do
so because this is a reference book for students, practitioners and
teachers who may have different views based on their own Qi Men
systems and lineages.

-- 472 of 810 --

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 461
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
F
While we will attempt to modify some of the information that are glaringly
inapplicable (For instance, we use cars now in lieu of horse carriages),
we choose not to alter the content too much in order to preserve its
original essence.
You will need to make use of your judgment and also some creativity
to make full sense of the information. Of course, guidance from your Qi
Men teacher would be a necessity to interpret this section effectively.
Experience plays a very large role in coming up with your own set of
interpretations based on these texts as a guide.
For instance, you may see a paragraph of the text that says:
“A crippled man is seen with a bottle of wine
and you’ll hear the sound of drumbeats from
the Northwest. After six months, you will receive
fortune from a woman. If you also see a snake
escaping from a well, this indicates that a person
in white outfit will bestow you with farm animals.”
If you take this literally, such occurrence is going to be rare if you live in
the city. You don’t see snakes on the streets of city. This phenomena or
image can be interpreted this way – snake could be related to items like
cables, pipes, trains, railway tracks or anything that resembles a snake.
It could mean the South East direction as the animal sign Snake belongs
to the South East sector. Farm animals may mean domestic animals or
pets in the modern world. Sound of drumbeats may be festive music.
Cripple man may refer to someone who have hurt his leg or someone
who is limping because of a recent injury.

In short, you need to make use of your own judgment in coming up with
the interpretation. To observe these occurrences of evidence, you need
to travel in the direction as indicated by the special formation - after
the specific chart of the formation is chosen. For example, a “Heavenly
Heart at the Open Door” sector of the Qi Men Chart you selected may
appear in the West area.
This means that when you travel West (at the hour prescribed by that
chart), you will come across the occurrence of evidence as described
in the ancient text. And if you do see any signs of these occurrences,
they serve to tell you that the special Qi Men structure is now active.
And shortly after, the outcome (positive or negative) as prescribed by
the special formation can be expected.
And for most of this section, you are required to know the difference
between the Host and the Guest. This is because each chart can be
good or bad, depending on which side are you on. Are you the Guest or
are you the Host. One is proactive and the other is responsive.

The Heavenly Grass 天蓬星
The Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 Star represents vast knowledge and
wisdom, but it is tainted with a crooked streak that catalyzes traits like
theft and robbery. It denotes one that marches forward to take success
and destiny into his or her own hands.
The Water is cold and dark, and it favors the Yin and fears the Yang.
This is the nature of Winter, the season where the Water is prosperous.
The Water should have its flow and destination; otherwise disaster will
ensue as water without a destination is like the flood that formed after
a downpour, which cannot be halted easily. The Heavenly Grass 天蓬星
is considered a malevolent star. It is also known as the Criminal Warlord
Star 盜星, and it also represents a person who does great (and often
dangerously big) things [做大事的人]. The Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 is
also, in a way regarded as a volatile Wealth Star 財星, and has both fast
upsides and downsides of money.
The Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 is also known as the Greedy Wolf Star 貪狼
星, which corresponds to the Kan 坎 Palace (1) at North, belonging to
the Yang polarity. It is said that where the Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 falls
into, it is better to construct city and placate the border, recruit soldiers
and defend firmly, and one will emerge victorious in battle in spring and
summer. Soldiers will perish in higher number for the seasons of autumn
and winter. It’s advantageous for the Host and disadvantageous for the
Guest under the influence of this star. It’s disadvantageous for marriage
or relational matters as well as undertaking a house construction or
house repair. Operating business will end up in loss of money and
inventory. It’s only auspicious when the Life Door meets with the Bing
and Yi along with the Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 Star.

When the Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 is present, it would be better to enforce
measure to prevent theft, and tighten up the security and employ defense
by constructing a citywall or barrier and recruit soldiers for protection. It
is also of great advantage to execute a great event as this star is similar
to an underworld warlord, loving big gatherings and assemblies of the
heroic in nature. But where the structures are negative, such gatherings
or parties will be afflicted by theft or financial loss and disease. The
Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 is a Thief God and it represents murder or theft.
According to ancient texts:
• 	Those who encountered the Grass Star will emerge victorious
in legal disputes
• 	It is auspicious to harness the positive energies of the Grass
Star in spring and summer, and inauspicious to use this Star
in autumn and winter
• 	It is acceptable to use the Grass Star for marriage or travel,
and will also bring no harm if this Star is used for burial or
construction purposes - provided the structure is positive
• 	Should the Life Door 生門 occupy the same Palace as the
Bing 丙 and Yi 乙 Palaces, then auspicious and positive
outcomes may be expected

剋應歌訣 Songs
歌曰：
天蓮主事宜秋冬，用訟安邊春夏功；
嫁娶俱亡移徒火，入官險到門達兇。
商貧埋葬可行否，相合曰奇門亦難通；
加土利主水利客，相旺時方事可成。
又曰：
爭訟庭競遇天蓮，勝捷威名萬里同；
春夏用之皆大利，秋冬用此半為凶。
嫁娶遠行多不利，葬埋修造亦嫌空；
須得生門同丙已，用之萬事得昌榮。
It is said that:
This star is disadvantageous for activities such as traveling, marriage,
funeral or construction work. It also denotes inauspiciousness for
taking on the officer title as well.
When it meets with the Life Door and the 3 Wonders (Bing, Yi and
Ding), it is an indication of a prosperous turn and positive result.
This star is auspicious in the spring and summer seasons, but not
in the autumn and winter period, where its auspiciousness would
be diminished.
The Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 is also called the Zi Qin 子禽.

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 481
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
芮
Grain
F
The Heavenly Grain 天芮星
The Heavenly Grain is also known as the Huge Door, which role is to
govern the right and wrong. Even though it denotes disease and danger,
for wealth or making friends, it is favorable.
The Heavenly Grain Star is known as the Star of Disease and Illness.
It is an inauspicious star. It also governs disputes, arguments and
disagreements. It also represents the location or position of a large
troop, working as a big unit or team, or a huge camp. It also resembles
the complexity of a governmental organization. It is a star that represents
illness in Qi Men and it also symbolizes students.
It’s also known as the Huge Door Star 巨門星, a Yin polarity Star, and
corresponds to the Kun Palace (2) in the Southwest.
When the Heavenly Grain is present, it’s good for socializing, recruiting
solders for defense (or hiring new talents) and to take on the role of an
educator or to be a student of a wise person. It’s disadvantageous for
army deployment, marriage, and lawsuit, house moving or repairing a
building. If the Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 is in the Fan Yin position, this
means that any new disease can be remedied by a cure, and old stubborn
ones will die out on their own.

482 Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
芮
Grain
F
According to ancient texts:
• 	This Star is auspicious in autumn and winter, and
inauspicious if used in spring and summer
• 	The Heavenly Grain Star is auspicious for establishing a
connection or relationship with others, but only in its passive
form
• 	The Grain Star is unsuitable for proactive endeavors and
pursuits, as well as constructing graves; otherwise, one will
suffer from endless problems
• 	Where the Grain Star is seen, be mindful of robbery, theft
and other incidents that could terrify the younger members of
the family
• 	Even those who harness the energies of the Grain Star will
not benefit much, where fortune is concerned

It is advantageous for activities such as knowledge attainment and
socializing but expect inverse outcome if the Heavenly Grain is
applied for travel, health matters and burial preparation.
This star is beneficial in the autumn and winter season, but not
during the spring and summer period. Even with the presence of
Envoy, the positive effects will be difficult to establish.
The Heavenly Grain is also known as Zi Cheng 子成

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 497
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
沖
Destructor
F
The Heavenly Destructor 天沖星
The Heavenly Destructor indicates an aggressive temperament and
irrational action. It is characterized as forthright and sincere. The
definition of success or failure to this star is not in accordance to what
is generally expected of from the public. This star believes in behaving
cruel to be kind, to love is to be tough and to control is to protect. It has
a unique self-identity or idea of kindness and what good fortune means
and they are not the ordinary standards that everyone seems to favor.
The Heavenly Destructor exudes high moral values and has the kindness
to assist others, albeit in its own - frequently harsh - way. Fast-paced
in everything it does, it can be easily irritated when things go awry. It
bodes well with the agriculture industry. As it is not as auspicious as the
Heavenly Heart, the Heavenly Ambassador, or the Heavenly Assistant,
the Heavenly Destructor is a moderately auspicious Star.
It is also called the Fortune Treasurer Star, a Yang polarity Star, which
corresponds to the Zhen 震 Trigram (3), the place that the Heavenly
Destructor resides in. This star dictates that it is better to strike first,
as the initiators have upper hand in battles, revenge, and socializing.
You will attain greater success in the spring and summer season, as
opposed to autumn and winter. It is disadvantageous for marriage,
house moving and construction, or business. If it falls in the same
palace as the auspicious Rest 休門, Open 開門, Life Door 生門, all
matters could develop smoothly and positively.
With the Heavenly Destructor, it is advantageous to start off battle
and attack from the front line. It is also good for charity or donation
activities.

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 513
奇
門
遁
甲
寶

輔
Assistant
F
The Heavenly Assistant 天輔星
The Heavenly Assistant represents obtaining fame and success in the
scholarly and educational fields. It's favorable to learn from a teacher
and advantageous to approach an imperial officer. It also denotes
favorable luck for operating a business, cultural attainment, house repair,
marriage, building relationships, networking, teaching and traveling.
The Heavenly Assistant is related to art, culture and education. It is
an auspicious star and is also known as the Literary Arts Star, and
corresponds to the Xun 巽 Palace (4) in the Southeast.
With the Heavenly Assistant Star, it is auspicious for most matters - travel,
business, marriage, house repair or moving and especially education.
This star is favorable when you’re sitting for higher educational exams
and for cultural learning. Use it during spring and summer, as it is more
favorable, especially for childbirth.
According to ancient texts:
• 	The Assistant Star is suitable to be used during all four
seasons of the year
• 	The Assistant Star may be used for all endeavors, from travel
to burial, as they will proceed smoothly and produce positive
outcomes
• 	This Star may be used by those starting a new job or
migrating to another country, as one will prosper accordingly
in terms of fame and fortune

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 527

Bird
F
The Heavenly Bird 天禽星
The Heavenly Bird is pure, and it denotes one with the talent for
formulating plans that bring people together for a common purpose.
This star is righteous and principled centered. It has great leadership.
The Earth nurtures all living things. The Heavenly Bird is also the Leader
Star, a Yang polarity Star. It is associated with the Chastity Star 廉貞星
and corresponds with the Central Palace of the Luo Shu.
In Qi Men, the Heavenly Bird always boards and lodges with the
Heavenly Grain star. This is the reason why the Heavenly Bird lives
together with the Heavenly Grain.
With the Heavenly Bird, it's advantageous for travel, meeting with
superiors (and asking for favors), pursuing fame, beginning and
operating a business and pursuing relationship goals. This star is an all-
rounded star for a myriad of activities. In most cases, all is smooth and
auspicious in all four seasons.
According to ancient texts:
• 	The Bird Star can be used for a diverse range of endeavors,
including travel, trade and commerce, as well as launching a
new business
• 	The Bird Star may also be used for burial related purposes
• 	Those who harness the energies of the Bird Star will enjoy
the support and assistance of noble people, who will be of
great help to one, especially in times of need

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 541
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
心
Heart
F
The Heavenly Heart 天心星
The Military Arts Star, has great leadership and thus able to manage
wealth and lead an army with ease. A true leader that serves, it also
possesses the gentle and delicate skill to care for the hurt and diseased.
One will also obtain the public recognition and approval as a leader of
Heaven.
The Heavenly Heart is a Yang polarity Star. It corresponds with the Qian
乾 Palace (6) at the Northwest direction. The Qian represents the leader
or father – and as such, the Heavenly Heart possesses the talents of a
leader, which includes the capability to oversee matters in the military
and finance, heal and cure diseases, and a natural in strategy and
tactics. It is a very auspicious star.
According to ancient texts:
• 	The Heart Star is more suitable to be used in the autumn and
winter seasons for wealth-related pursuits, starting a new job,
construction, spiritual and religious activities, as well as trade
and commerce
• 	The preceding activities should be avoided in spring and
summer
• 	The Heart Star is best used for seeking medical cures and
treatments for ailments
• 	If the Heart Star resides together with the Life Door 生門, it
will bring about positive outcomes in all four seasons of the
year
• 	This Star heralds fresh starts and new beginnings, where
one’s endeavors will proceed smoothly
• 	The Heart Star is also suitable for moving into a new
residence or burial

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 555
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
柱
Pillar
F
The Heavenly Pillar 天柱星
The Heavenly Pillar is also known as the Broken Soldier Star, and
it denotes war, carnage, victory and glory. It calls for one to always
remain calm and cast away their fear, even in the face of danger or in
unmanageable situations. This star boosts the skills that entail a sense
of destruction and damage.
This inauspicious star, a Yin polarity star, has an affinity with blood and
havoc and it represents the need to shape the law, redesign culture and
influence society. It corresponds to the Dui 兌 Palace (7) in the West
sector.
Where the Heavenly Pillar star resides, it is auspicious to repair the base
camp, train and recruit soldiers, prepare the defense battalion, military
preparation and it is also good for camouflaging one’s movements.
It is unsuitable for distant traveling, starting off battle, meeting and
approaching high level officers for favors, house moving and business
activities.
With the help of the Heavenly Pillar star, it is advantageous for embarking
on lawsuits, executing industrial espionage and for questioning suspects.
It is inauspicious for business and investments, both of which could lead
to the death of troops, fortune loss and circumstances of unexpected
outcome.

The Heavenly Ambassador governs progress and makes lives bloom
and vigor begins to flow.
Citizens are happy as the country’s literacy is high and the economy
level is healthy and strong, both of which an indicator for a blooming
country.
The Earth is the material that denotes life and vitality. The Heavenly
Ambassador is also called the Left Assistant Star 左輔星, which governs
crucial financial matters that touch the lives of everything on Earth. This
star corresponds to the Gen 艮 Palace (8) in the Northeast and it is a
Yang polarity Star.
With the help of the Heavenly Ambassador, it is suitable for developing a
country and fostering a safe environment to live in. In the modern context,
this star is capable of building a business empire. It also denotes good
outcomes for business, marriage, house repair and moving and meeting
Noble people. This star is auspicious for most of the time, and it can be
used in every season.
The Heavenly Ambassador’s location signify a talent with ability so
strong and potent, it could take on great task and create an empire.
Good outcome can be expected in everything you do.

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 583
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
英
Hero
F
The Heavenly Hero 天英星
With the presence of the Heavenly Hero, your sense of bravery and
courage will be ignited, like a burning fire. This spirit can radiate through
the whole world and it also radiates within the minds of those whose
lives you touch.
Also known as the Right Assistant Star, this Yin polarity star corresponds
with the Li Palace (9). As the Fire element, it shows a certain quality of
malevolent energy in its characteristics. Hence, despite being imaged as
the Sun in the middle of the day, shining brightly, it has a more volatile and
unstable side to it. It’s emotional and energetic. As such, it is considered
a slightly inauspicious star.
The Right Assistant Star corresponds to the Li 離 Gua of the South
direction. It is advantageous for meeting with Noble people (asking for
assistance) and for planning and strategizing. But it is not beneficial for
long-distance travel, house moving and repair, business operation or
asking for fortune as you’re likely to suffer from financial loss or unwanted
outcome as your consequences. This star is heroic and rowdy – as it is
bad in details and management.
Where this star is located, it is advantageous to start planning, designing
and creating a system or idea to achieve a goal. You may also meet with
your superiors or Noble people to ask and receive favors. It is also useful
when you’re running a consultancy firm.

1. Destiny Analysis
When the Heavenly Assistant star is timely, and receiving one of the
Three Nobles (Yi, Bing or Ding), you will be bestowed with an excellent
academic achievement and respectable reputation. If the Heavenly
Assistant is untimely, chances are you will end up as a monk, librarian
or just a poor scholar.
When the Heavenly Destructor comes into a timely stage, it would be
auspicious for armies standing by on defense.
The Heavenly Bird is located in the middle of the Five Palaces, and when
it receives the Three Nobles (Yi, Bing or Ding) or an auspicious Door;
this person will take on the position as the leader of a region, or as the
highest ranking officer.
When the Heavenly Hero sits in the Zhen Palace (3), this person is likely
to assume high ranking position in a governmental organization. When
it resides in the Li Palace with the right noble Stems, this person will
turn out to be a courteous and polite gentleman. But if it is met with the
wrong stems, this is a greedy, cruel and witless individual.
If the Heavenly Pillar is in the Dui Palace (7), this person will make a
good civil officer. If this star falls on the West area, it is in a timely status,
and this person will be blessed with exceptional oratory, speaking skills
that can influence thousands. If this star is untimely or countered, then
this person is likely to turn up to be a con artist.
When the Heavenly Heart lands in the Li Palace (9), this person will
become a good doctor. He or she will be blessed with the right skills and
talent to heal others. With an auspicious Door, this individual will also
take on greater task and may one day end up as the pillar of strength
for his or her country. If this star falls into the Emptiness or the Enters
Graveyard, this person will end up as a disgrace, plagued with scandals
and will lead a life in a regrettable manner.

F
When the Heavenly Ambassador arrives in a Metal Palace or meets
with the Metal element components, the person can possess land and
properties, servants and lots of assets. If the star is countered, one will
dwell only in administrative work and enjoy an average life. If it falls in
the Dui Palace (7), this person will end up as the leader of society or
hold a superior position.
When the Heavenly Grain falls in a sector where it is countered,
and encounters an Auspicious Door, this person is likely to end up
as prosecutor or as an officer in the law or judicial field. If there are
negative Stem structures, this person will spend a lot of time plotting
and scheming, probably on evil wrongdoings, and his or her wealth will
not last long.
When the Heavenly Grass falls in the same palace of the Hour Stem,
this person will become a general or officer, which duty involved
defending the country’s borders. Otherwise, he or she will grow up to
be a soldier or a famous thief. When it meets at the Kan Palace (1) with
an Auspicious Door, he or she will end up as a person with inclination
to do evil deeds.

2. The 9 Stars and 8 Doors Combination Effect
on Character
When the Open Door 開門 meets with the Heavenly Heart Star, it is
slightly auspicious, and this person will likely to become a doctor,
astrologer, healer or a high ranking manager. When met with the Death
and the Trap Door, he or she will end up as a laborer.
The Life Door 生門 meets with the Heavenly Ambassador that belongs
to the Earth element, hence produces Metal. This is called the God of
Earth. Otherwise, this person will end up a farm laborer.
The Rest Door 休門 meets with the Heavenly Grass 天蓬星 that belongs
to Water, and in the Strong stage. It indicates one that will end up as a
soldier or a defense officer. If it is met with the Death and Trap status,
the person will become a coroner or forensic officer or a thief.
The Harm Door 傷門 meets with the Heavenly Destructor, which belongs
to the Wood, and in the timely stage, indicates a person that is likely to
take on the role of a military officer or a leader of a network. If it resides
with the Weak and Death, this person will end up as a soldier.
The Delusion Door 杜門 meets with the Heavenly Assistant, which
belongs to the Wood, and in the timely stage, indicates a person that will
become a good but poor scholar. If met with the Grave and Extinction
status, this person will become a monk or spiritual guru.
The Scenery Door 景門 meets with the Heavenly Hero, which belongs
to the Fire, and in the timely stage is destined for great things. A life of
glamour and fame. Otherwise, if it lands on an untimely palace coupled
with a negative structure, it denotes one that will lead a mediocre,
lackluster life.
When the Heavenly Assistant comes into the Prosperous stage, you will
be bestowed with excellent academic achievement and high reputation.
Otherwise, chances are you will end up as a poor scholar, roadside artist
or a part time painter.

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 609
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
G
The 8 Deities 八神
Introduction
The Eight Deities (also known as the Eight Generals) in Qi Men comprise
the ‘universal energy’ or ‘spirit energy’ that is referred to in a Qi Men
chart.
These Eight Deities are sometimes also known as the “Eight Deception
Doors”. Similar to the extra terrestrials or spiritual beings in the ancient
hamanic divination systems, these Eight Deities were devised by the
ancient sages as the eight symbols to represent the mysterious forces of
our Universe that influence heaven-human interaction. The Eight Deities
govern the Spirit Realm that influences all things on Earth.
Though the concept of “Spirit Realm” sits comfortably in the constitution
of most religions, it is itself not the religion. Qi Men does not have any
religious associations.
While most religions focus on the well-being of inner life, the concept of
Spirit Realm in Qi Men is regarded as an external environment of energy.
It is independent from the natural world, but both the Spirit Realm and
the Natural world are in constant interaction with one another.
Through Qi Men, these two realms – Spirit and Natural - can consciously
communicate, connect and influence each other.
The Eight Deities act as symbols of Universal or Spiritual influence to a
Natural World situation. Its presence can indicate the good or ill fortune
of an event or an outcome.
Because the Spiritual Realm floats on the highest level of the Heaven –
Man – Earth realms, the Eight Deities is considered to have the highest
status among the rest of the inhabitants of these worlds.

-- 621 of 810 --

610 Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
G
Some people have wondered what these Eight Deities or Spirits look like.
It is said that those who are sensitive enough are especially receptive
to these “spirits”. However in Qi Men, what is commonly referred to as
spirits – the visible entities that can be felt by some highly-sensitive
individuals - are in fact, souls, and not spirits.
Human beings, no matter how naturally sensitive and no matter how
much training they have undergone, can only see up until the “Astral”
realm. This is in fact somewhere slightly above in the energy fields of the
Human realm. It is also where the ‘souls’ reside. In reality, souls and the
residual energy of the Human life form do not linger in the Spirit Realm.
Of course, the more exceptionally advanced and trained practitioners of
spiritual arts can see further into the Spirit Realm, a higher energy plane
above the Humans.
The Eight Deities represent divine intervention in life. Some of the Eight
Deities offer protection or assistance while some offer “lessons” in the
form of misfortune and problems.
The Eight Deities in Qi Men are: Chief 直符, Surging Snake 騰蛇, Great
Moon 太陰, Six Harmony 六合, White Tiger 白虎, Black Tortoise 玄武,
Nine Earth 九地, and Nine Heaven 九天.
Originally, there were eleven Deities according to the ancient Qi Men
texts. But during the later dynasties, Qi Men scholars have merged the
White Tiger 白虎 with Grappling Hook 勾陳 and Black Tortoise 玄武 with
Red Phoenix 朱雀 and The Great Constant 太常 with the Heavenly Bird
天禽 together. So in the current Qi Men system, the line up of the Eight
Deities are :
1) Chief 直符
2) Surging Snake 騰蛇
3) Great Moon 太陰
4) Six Harmony 六合
5) Grappling Hook 勾陳
(Grappling Hook 勾陳 for Yang Dun, White Tiger 白虎 for Yin Dun)
6) Red Phoenix 朱雀
(Red Phoenix 朱雀 for Yang Dun, Black Tortoise 玄武 for Yin Dun)
7) Nine Earth 九地
8) Nine Heaven 九天

The arrangement of Eight Deities follows a specific order. Their
arrangement is not as complicated as that of the plotting of the Nine
Stars or Eight Doors. Its specific order depends mainly on whether the
chart is a Yin Dun or Yang Dun. The general rule is this: circular, forward
flow for Yang Dun after the Winter Solstice, circular reverse flow motion
for Yin Dun after the Summer Solstice; but either way the starting point
should always be at the Chief Deity.
The arrangement of Eight Deities is as follows:

Yin Dun Set: Anti-clockwise Flow
The Eight Deities, including the Chief, Surging Snake, Great Moon, Six
Harmony, White Tiger (Grappling Hook), Black Tortoise (Red Phoenix),
Nine Earth and Nine Heaven, are placed at the Spirit Plate of a Qi Men
chart. Take note that the White Tiger and Black Tortoise are used for Yin
Dun charts; they are replaced by Grappling Hook and Red Phoenix in
Yang Dun charts.

-- 625 of 810 --

614 Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
G
The Spirit Realm or the Universe Realm is known as the Deity Plate in Qi
Men. The main Deity in Deity Plate, which consists of the Eight Deities,
is called the Chief 值符, but oftentimes, it is also referred to as the Small
Leader 小值符. This distinction is necessary to differentiate it from the
Nine Stars Plate’s Lead Star which is called the Lead Star 大值符. The
Chinese terms are the same. But for English-speaking students, I’ve
taken the liberty to use a different term to make it easier for reference.
Why ancient Chinese scholars used the same terminology for different
stars remains a question that perplexes many of us, including me.
The Eight Deities Plate can also be arranged in Yin Dun or Yang Dun
sequence. In the Yang Dun arrangement, the Eight Deities are arranged
in the following sequence: Chief, Surging Snake, Great Moon, Six
Harmony, Grappling Hook, Red Phoenix, Nine Earth and Nine Heaven.
In the Yin Dun arrangement, the Eight Deities are arranged as follows:
Chief Nine Heaven, Nine Earth, Black Tortoise, White Tiger, Six Harmony,
Great Moon and Surging Snake. Eight Deities are arranged in a fixed
order. Yang Dun runs clockwise, Yin Dun runs counter clockwise.

Eight Deities in Yin Dun (Reverse Flow - Anticlockwise)
Once the place of Chief 值符 is determined, the rest of the deities will be
arranged in line with either the Yin Dun and Yang Dun format around the
Qi Men Chart. The location of the Chief 值符 is also the location of the
Lead Star 值符星.
There are two schools of Qi Men “chart plotting” - The Rotating Palace
轉宮法 	Zhuan Gong Fa and the Flying Palace 飛宮法 	Fei Gong Fa
Method. In the Flying Palace Method, there are 9 Deities instead of 8.
The Nine Deities are: Chief 直符, Surging Snake 騰蛇, Great Moon 太
陰, Six Harmony 六合, Grappling Hook 勾陳, Great Constant 太常, Red
Phoenix 朱雀, Nine Earth 九地 and Nine Heaven 九天.
As there are only Eight Trigrams on Earth, the School of Rotating Palace
abides by the principle of “The Door Not Entering the Middle Palace
門不入中宮,” and it excludes the Great Constant, matching the Eight
Trigrams to just Eight Deities. The reason behind this stems from the
understanding that the Eight Trigrams are used to represent the eight
directions and twenty-four solar terms. And together with the cycle
of Sixty Pillars, the Eight Deities are able to influence the Heaven and
Man’s activities on Earth. This way, the Eight Deities, representing the
Spirit Realm, can be used to influence time, space and events.

符
Chief
Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 619
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
G
Chief 直符
Introduction
Chief, the Heavenly Yi 天乙 rules on life and death;
All evil vanishes, when the Heavenly Qi arrives.
Chief is the head of the Eight Deities and the Nine Stars; so it is
recognized as the Leader 值符. In Qi Men Dun Jia, the term 值 denotes
one that is on duty. Hence, it is also the Deity on Duty.
The original element of the Chief Deity is Fire and it belongs in the
central position. It is the Deity that governs and creates all things on
Earth. Evil will be subdued and eliminated wherever the Chief resides.
This deity is one of the most auspicious of all the Eight Deities.
Even the Great White Geng Metal 太白庚金, the most ferocious of all
Sha Qi will be subdued when it meets with the Chief Deity. This is
because the Chief is of the Fire element. And the Great White Geng
Metal (太白庚金) is Metal element. Fire counters Metal.
The Chief Star exerts most of its positive Qi under a good
formation. Even if it lands on a negative formation, it will not exert
any negative Qi.
As the Heaven begins from Jia 甲 and the Earth begins with Zi 子,
the Chief is the head or leader of all the Six Jias. Hence it is the most
benevolent of all the 8 Deities.
In terms of shape, it is square-like while in terms of colour, it is
represented by yellow or white. Its representative numbers are one and
eight.
For personnel forecasting, the Chief refers to the current leadership or
the leader with direct powers on site or in a particular situation. The
Chief also indicates protection, assistance, head, leadership, high-
status, elevated ranking, famous people and Noble positions.

-- 631 of 810 --

620 Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium
符
Chief
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
G
Although the Chief Deity is the most auspicious deity, its influence will be
greatly reduced when it enters Emptiness 空亡. There is a line from the
ancient text that says “值符逢空，年命不保", which tells us that “when
Chief enters Emptiness 空亡, the Life cannot be preserved.”
If we use a physical item to represent the Chief Deity, then it is likely
to be something high-end, expensive, and luxurious, denoting genuine
high status, good quality and sophistication. If we use a person from
a company to represent the Chief Deity, then he/she will likely be the
leader, the boss or manager or someone who is in charge.
If the Chief lands on the 4 Cardinal Palaces 四正宮 (1, 3, 7 and 9), it
may indicate the principal positions; where if it lands in the four Auxiliary
Palaces 四維宮 (8, 4, 2 and 6), it may indicate the deputy positions.
The Sixth Palace, the Heaven Palace, would be an exception because it
stands for the head and hence, indicates a principal position. Moreover,
the Chief can also be used to represent a boss, proctor, referee, plaintiff,
money lender, bank, market situation, defensive side of a war, in addition
to other.

Snake
G
Surging Snake 騰蛇
Originally as the God of Fire, Surging Snake is the master of
deception and panic.
With the vicious tongue playing a double game, the lies would
become the truth.
The Surging Snake belongs to the Yin Earth element. It is known as the
Deity of Deception 虛詐之神. Its origin palace is in the Southern Bing
and Ding Fire. Among the Five Elements, it has the nature of both Yin
Fire and Yin Earth. The weird and treacherous temperament makes
it the darkest natured Yin Deity of the group. It indicates a two faced
nature, and the tendency to deceive people with a vicious tongue.
As the master of disputes over ownership of land, wood, grain and
crops, it loves to scheme and mislead. The people, things and items at
the position of the Surging Snake are generally ethereal, outrageously
glamorous and glittering, or elongated in shape, with red or white color.
The associated numbers are usually two and eight.
The Surging Snake is flexible and poisonous. As the master of terrifying
and weird things, it governs freakish and wildish fantasies. The persons
influenced by the Surging Snake will be cunning and erratic. Items will
get rotten and decayed.
The Surging Snake is flexible and poisonous. As the master of terrifying
and weird things, it governs freakish and wildish fantasies. The persons
influenced by the Surging Snake will be cunning and erratic. Items will
rot, fester and decay under the Surging Snake.
Surging Snake represents mystery, darkness and the uncanny. Its
nature is dark, strange, cruel and untruthful. It represents lies and
worldly attachments.

Wherever the Useful God of the Qi Men is in the location of the Surging

The only few possible positive outcomes for the Surging Snake are
when the topic of discourse is related to the occult or spiritual practices.
Then this represents good fortune. It can imply that the person is often
interested in the mysterious, non-conventional wisdom.

Moon
G
Great Moon 太陰
Originally the Deity of Blessing, the Great Moon governs one’s
virtue received from the ancestors.
Favors the darkness and concealment, it is best for covert
operations and ambush.
The Great Moon belongs to Yin Metal. It is regarded as the Deity of
Blessings 陰祐之神, which brings about protection, comfort and safety. It
is particularly strong for matters representing femininity or Yin energy. This
deity denotes gentle emotions, feelings, thoughts and intrinsic value.
People, things and items in the position of Great Moon generally indicate
those that are private or away from public attention. It represents closed-
door events, behind-the-scenes preparation or activities, planning and
resting. The dominant color is white, the shape or state is soft and the
number is four or nine.
The Great Moon favors darkness and concealment. With Great Moon
in the positive position, it is best to take refuge, go into hiding, retire or
rest. If an attack is necessary, then it’s good for setting up an ambush.
It indicates plotting, being trapped or being in hiding.
The Great Moon represents what is hidden and ambiguous. In a
positive setting, it favors conspiracy as well as cattiness, cruelty and
ruthlessness. It is characterized as darkness, shadow, gloom and
insidiousness; the concerned person is restrained, introverted and quiet
who likes doing things in a stealth mode.
The Great Moon is usually taken as an auspicious deity. If one’s Useful
God is with the Great Moon, it often indicates the assistance secretly
offered by a Noble person. It can represent a hidden mentor or a
tender loving guardian angel. On the other hand, where the formation
is negative, the image can also negatively indicate that one is sinister,
astute, ruthless and with the tendency to conceal his or her true nature.
In short, each symbol has a dual nature to imply both the good and bad
outcomes.

Harmony
G
Six Harmony 六合
Known as The Deity of Harmony, the Six Harmony is versatile and
amendable in handling personal affairs.
Deals and negotiations will go smoothly with festive weddings and
marriages.
The Six Harmony, with an amiable and warm nature, represents The
Deity of Harmony 和合之神. It governs relationships and personal affairs.
It is the master of union-related and relational matters such as marriage,
intimacy, connection, joy, match-making and bonding. It also acts as an
intermediary in arguments and represents evidence in a dispute case. In
a positive location, the Six Harmony favors negotiations, discussions,
match-making, marriages and as well as peace-making.
The Six Harmony is a Guardian Deity 議衛之神 with a calm and cheerful
character. Being tough on the outside but sensitive at heart, it becomes
the master of marriages, transactions, intermediary and matters relating
to match-making. Its proper position favors negotiations, transactions,
marriages and weddings, mediation and production.
There’s a story as to how the name “Six” Harmony came about. The
original birth location of this Deity is in the East. In the East location,
there are two stems – Jia 甲 and Yi 乙 Wood. Jia is Yang 陽, representing
the older brother and Yi is Yin 陰, representing the younger sister. In Qi
Men, the Jia Wood is the Grand Marshall . Geng 庚 Metal is the enemy.
In warring times one of the strategies used to turn enemies into allies
was to use “marriage” as a weapon. Jia offers Yi Wood to Geng Metal
for marriage. (In the study of the Ten Heavenly Stems combination, Yi
Wood ‘combines’ with Geng Metal). By marrying Jia Wood’s sister to the
Geng Metal, the defense in the East is guaranteed. So starting the count
from Yi Wood to Ji Earth, the ordinal number is six. Therefore the name
of this star is called the “Six Harmony”.

Harmony
G
The Six Harmony deity has a mild, gentle, soothing and loving
character. It loves to be the match-maker and persuader of a marriage
or negotiation. The Six Harmony enjoys happy occasions, celebrations,
banquets and happy weddings. Its favorite colors are red and yellow
and the associated numbers are 6 and 7.
The Six Harmony is usually regarded as an auspicious deity. This is
because it encourages bonding and unions. According to its implied
meaning, Six Harmony consists of at least two combined parties;
therefore, it can be used to indicate many parties. In some cases of
analysis, The Six Harmony can act as the Useful God to represent marriage,
intermediaries, brokers, lost pedestrians and fleeing prisoners.

White Tiger 白虎/ Grappling Hook 勾陳
Known as the Ferocious Metal God, the White Tiger causes fierce
fights, bringing about pain and harm.
With its upholding paws, the world will become dark; with mighty
powers that everyone fears.
The White Tiger belongs to the Metal element. Its origin is in the West
and it is known as the Demon Deity 煞神. It represents the enforcement
of law and order. Being ferocious and aggressive, it is the master of
armies and wars, fights and murders, deaths, injuries and diseases,
traffic accidents and the enforcement of administrative laws, weapons
and security matters.
Its image indicates roads, pathways, transport, sensitive or classified
information, battles, authority, bloodshed and dirty money. The White
Tiger is short-tempered, determined, strong willed and well-educated.
It is not afraid of bloodshed and pain. In fact, it’s the master of
inflicting pain.
The White Tiger is has a very fierce and stubborn nature - coupled with
a sharp tongue. Being ferocious and aggressive, it brings quarrels,
fratricidal struggles and family disputes. On the other hand, if favorable
formations with Auspicious Stars, Auspicious Door and Auspicious
Structure are present, the White Tiger can indicate one who is fair and
just, who is not afraid to stand up for righteous principles and fight for
the oppressed.

The Grappling Hook (勾陳)
The Grappling Hook has an eye for everything competitive and
aggressive, and it governs land and litigation.
For commencement or resting, it will denote instability and a
confused mind
The Grappling Hook, a Yin Earth 陰土 Deity is hidden under the White
Tiger. The Grappling Hook Deity can produce panics, mysterious and
sinister events and spread rumors to deceive or frighten people. People,
things and items in the position of Grappling Hook are generally military
or war related, or in the absence of those, these objects are usually
scary or sinister looking. The appearance is of sharp forms in green or
white with the representative numbers of seven or five.
The Grappling Hook is known as the Cloud Deity 雲神. It has a
contentious and unfaithful character. It is the master of land, lawsuits,
sojourns and harvests. The Grappling Hook is a Fierce Deity with a
stubborn nature and malicious tongue. Being ferocious and aggressive,
it is the master of fights and wars, assassinations, trauma, injuries and
diseases, traffic accidents and great misfortunes.

G
Red Phoenix 朱雀
Known as the Thief Deity, the Black Tortoise is involved in
wickedness and treachery.
Clever and crafty, the Black Tortoise is a master of trickery and
distraction.
The Black Tortoise belongs to the Water Element. It is known as the
God of Minor Offences 小盜之神 or the Theft Deity 盜神. With the
most powerful Yin Qi in the North, it is also referred to in some ancient
texts, as the Rain Deity 雨神, in charge of pure Yin Water. Being fond
of stealing, Black Tortoise is the master of thieves, fugitives, tricks and
even adultery.
The Black Tortoise is quick-tongued in argument, mischievous and in
charge of wind, cloud and rain water. The Black Tortoise represents
both the good and the bad - thieves, villains, policemen, special tactics
squad and prisoners. If the Black Tortoise is found in the same palace
as the Xin 辛 Stem, it represents a habitual offender.
The Black Tortoise is an immoral deity, governing lust, libido, dark
secrets, adultery, affairs or forbidden sex. It represents dissolute and
improper behaviors, indignity, greed for money and a phony character.
The Red Phoenix Deity is hidden under the Black Tortoise Deity. The
two are respectively placed in the South and the North, separated by
the Water and Fire elements. Both are considered a close pair. The Red
Phoenix is the Fire Deity 火神 in the South. It is the master of civilization,
debate and propaganda. If it is supported with a positive formation,
this Deity governs promotions and political wins. If it is surrounded
by a negative formation it denotes quarrels, war of words, scolding
or burned-out relationships. People, things and items in the position
of the Black Tortoise are generally related to medicine or witchcraft,
diseases, death mourning and the loss of wealth. Its shape is not round,
with faults; edgy or irregular. The colors are red and black with the
representative numbers of four or nine.

G
Nine Earth 九地
Known as the Deity of the Land, Nine Earth is of great and
Noble virtue.
With a gentle and quiet character, she is the mother of all
things on earth.
The Nine Earth belongs to Yin Earth and it is known as the Mother of
Earth 萬物之母. She possesses great virtue, is kind and has a gentle
and quiet character to nurture all things. As the symbol of Yin, the Nine
Earth is extremely caring, compassionate humble and amiable and is
respectful of all living things.
On the other hand, the Nine Earth Deity is in charge of the critical
matters of life and death. Therefore, it is at times considered both good
and bad in a Qi Men analysis. Kun 坤 contains Yi 乙 and Gui 癸; the
ordinal number from Yi to Gui is Nine; hence, the name, Nine Earth.
The position of Nine Earth favors troops in ambush, defense, long-term
habitation, sowing of the land, farming and local development.
All things will go smoothly in spring and summer, but adverse situations
arrive in autumn and winter. Its proper position favors concealment,
espionage, defense (rather than attack) and acquisition of passive
income. Nine Earth indicates steadiness, antiquity, dignity, collection,
delays, traps set by the villains, concealment and premeditation.
On most occasions, the Nine Earth is regarded as an auspicious deity.
Because of its steadiness, it can also be taken as the symbol for long
duration and endurance. The position of the Nine Earth favors defense by
stationed troops, sowing and farming. For the development or investment
on real estate and businesses, the Nine Earth is not only auspicious at
one point in time - it favors long-term and stable development.
The Nine Earth fears entering into Graveyard 入墓. Spring and Summer
will bring fortunes; Autumn and Winter will denote misfortune. People,
things and items in the location of the Nine Earth Deity are generally
concerned with seasonable issues, including medicine, divination,
morality, elderly women, cloth, and wellness. The Nine Earth appears to
be thick with a handle; the color is black and the representative number
is either two or eight.

G
Nine Heaven 九天
Known as the Old Father Deity, Nine Heaven is the relentless head
of all things.
With the force of strong, marching troops, it is the Deity of courage
and leadership.
The Nine Heaven is the supreme father of Earth and the Defense Deity
威捍之神. It is energetic, vibrant and motivated. The Nine Heaven
governs continuous and never ending improvement and personal
success. This deity has a strong, charismatic and active personality. It
is derived from the Metal of Qian 乾 Gua . Qian Gua in the theory of
Na Jia that contains both Jia 甲 and Ren 壬. From Jia; using the ordinal
number and counting to Ren壬, you’ll get the number 9. Hence the
name Nine Heaven.
Things or matters in the location of the Nine Heaven are usually
positive, just and fortunate. This deity governs honesty, sincerity and
righteousness. Its appearance is round or nearly round with hard quality;
the colors are red and white with the number of one or six.
The Nine Heaven favors the systematizing, organizing of teams and
long distance travels by plane. The image indicates a noisy situation,
excitement and stimulation. The initiative actions imply much discussion
and possible disturbances and troubles.
The Nine Heaven can help one achieve career advancement, improve
in character and personality, execute (rather than planning), meet with
great mentors and facilitate business deals.
If the Useful God is located with the auspicious Nine Heaven, this
formation will favor active starts and execution of grand plans. In terms
of traveling, it is suitable to go abroad by air. Therefore, Nine Heaven can
also represent flight. Similarly, if the travel is with Nine Earth, it indicates
subway, tunnels through the mountain or passages through river bottom
and seabed.

In terms of one	· 	’s health conditions, if the Nine Heaven, the
Heavenly Grain Star 天芮星 and Death Door 死門 are in the
same palace with the Yearly Stem of the concerned person,
one will suffer from lingering diseases or die.

746 Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
H
格局 Structure 天三門、地四戶
Heavenly 3 Doors, Earthly 4 Doors
解說
Description
• To achieve the Heavenly 3 Doors combination, determine whether
the Month General 月將 is in the Hour Branch, and check if the three
combinations of the Cong Kui 從 魁 at the You 酉 Palace, the Xiao Ji
小吉at the Wei 未 Palace and the Great Minister 太沖at the Mao 卯
Palace are residing in the Hour Stem.
• These are auspicious positions for matters relating to professional
fields.
• When these positions are determined, you can embark on activities
such as collecting debts, business dealing, seeking fame, operating
a new business, asking for a promotion, or embarking on an outdoor
adventure. This formation favors Yang activities.
• The same Heavenly 3 Doors can also be applied to the Qi Men plates
to reap a “supportive” 相乘 effect. You need to first check if they are
in the similar and auspicious direction with one another. Also, the
auspicious outcome will only be revealed when it meets with the Open
開, Rest 休, Life 生 and Scenery 景 Door.
• For the Earthly 4 Doors, go through the Hour Branch and make sure
the Month Establish 月建 is in it. Then, find out the Remove 除, Danger
危, Stable 定 and Open 開 Day Officers positions as they denote
auspiciousness for matters relating to professional fields.
• The positive effects from the Earthly 4 Doors are hidden and concealed
from the public eyes, unlike the Heavenly 3 Doors’ benefits which
are characterized as open and transparent. Therefore, the Earthly 4
Doors are suitable for covert activities, soft launching a project, market
testing and of course, scheming.
• Where its locations are corresponding with the Rest 休, Delusion 杜,
Life 生 and Harm 傷 Doors, the Earthly 4 Doors will be extremely
auspicious.
- Rest Door 休門: It is suitable for entertainment and leisure activities,
reconciliation, private affairs
- Delusion Door 杜門: It is suitable for retreating or concealing yourself
from your opponents, concealing facts and keeping to a low profile.
- Life Door 生門: It represents a beneficial boost for any private and
confidential activities.
- Harm Door 傷門: It denotes successful outcome in scheming against
your enemies

Private Earthly Door
解說
Description
In general, the Private Earthly Door refers to the effect of the
Twelve Heavenly Generals 十二天將 have on the Day or Hour.
This combination can be streamed into the Day Private Earthly
Door 日地私門 and the Hour Private Earthly Door 時地私門, which
indicates effects for a day and an hour (or 2 hours standard time)
respectively.
For the Hour Private Earthly Door, the auspicious effect is shorter
but it is very pronounced.
When the Six Harmony 六合, the Great Yin 太陰 and the Great
Emptiness 天空 are with the Yang Noble, this combination will
bring about victory in all outward activities – such as marketing,
promotional activities, sales and product launches.
If the Six Harmony, the Great Yin and the Great Emptiness are
with the Yin Noble, it denotes success to all inward activities such
as financial management, cleaning up of accounts, tightening up
internal controls and improving operational processes.
The Yang Noble direction is beneficial for business operation, career
progress, competitions, persuasive skills and activities undertaken
in the open or out of the office. The Yin Noble direction, however, is
beneficial for private affairs, leisure time, reconciliation, and hidden
or concealed ventures.

Hour Stem Enters Grave
解說
Description
The following conditions explain Hour Stem Enters Grave:
- At the Bing Xu 丙戌 hour, Bing丙 is in the Heaven Plate and
resides in the Qian 乾 Palace (6) of the Earth Plate (As Xu 戌 is
in Qian, the Grave of Bing Fire is in Xu);
- At the Ren Chen 壬辰 hour, Ren 壬 is in the Heaven Plate and
resides in the Xun 巽 Palace (4) of the Earth Plate (As Chen 辰 is
in Xun, the Grave of Ren Water is in Chen);
- At the Gui Wei 癸末 hour, Gui癸 is in the Heaven Plate and
resides in the Kun 坤 Palace (2) of the Earth Plate (As Wei 末 is
in Kun, the Grave of Gui Water is in Wei);
- At the Wu Xu 戊戌 hour, Xu 戌 is in the Heaven Plate and resides
in the Qian 乾 Palace (6) of the Earth Plate (As Xu 戌 is in Qian,
the Grave of Wu Earth is in Xu);
- At the Ji Chou 己丑 hour, Ji 己 is in the Heaven Plate and resides
in the Gen 艮 Palace (8) of the Earth Plate (As Chou 丑 is in
Gen, the Grave of Ji Earth is in Chou);
- At the Ding Chou 丁丑 hour, Ding 丁 is in the Heaven Plate and
resides in the Gen 艮 Palace (8) of the Earth Plate (As Chou 丑
is in Gen, the Grave of Ding Fire is in Chou).
This formation denotes that the matter you seek, as represented by
the Hour Stem, will not be successful or as desirable. The Entering
Grave reduces at least half of the Stems’ vitality. If the Stem was
positive, its positive energies would have been reduced by a major
portion.

Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium 761
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
I
In Qi Men Dun Jia, when a specific time is selected and applied, the
practitioner can look for indicators from the natural environment to
confirm that the formation is now active. This is called the “Wai Ying 外
應" or the “Evidence Occurrences” in Qi Men.
This section describes the occurrences of “evidence” you will see in
your living environment that tell you that the special formations are now
activated. As these sections are transliterated from the ancient texts,
some of its descriptions may not at first make much sense to you, or
may even sound weird or illogical. But bear in mind that these original
texts were written in ancient times and much of what they saw in the
environment back then is no longer the same as today.
While the environment and culture have changed, the context or the
principle remains the same. What we need to do is to take the idea or
the concept and apply it to the modern setting.
I am tempted to translate and convert all the information here into my
view of how they are in the modern world, but have chosen not to do
so because this is a reference book for students, practitioners and
teachers who may have different views based on their own Qi Men
systems and lineages.
In our attempt to modify some of the information that are glaringly
inapplicable (For instance, we can no longer find horse carriages, but
cars), we choose not to alter the content too drastically in order to
preserve its original essence.
You will need to make use of your judgment and also some creativity
to make full sense of the information. Of course, guidance from your Qi
Men teacher would be imperative to interpret this section effectively.
Experience also plays a very large role in coming up with your own set
of interpretations as these texts serve only as a guide for you.

-- 773 of 810 --

762 Qi Men Dun Jia Compendium
奇
門
遁
甲
寶
鑑
I
For instance, you may see a line of the texts that says ‘You will see a
Snake biting a Pig’. If you take this literally, such occurrence is going to
be rare if you live in the city. You certainly don’t see snakes or pigs on
the streets of New York. This phenomena or image can be interpreted
this way – snake could be related to items like cables, pipes, trains,
railway tracks or anything that resembles a serpent. It could mean the
South East direction as the animal sign Snake belongs to the South East
sector. Likewise, a pig may not necessarily refer to the actual animal
itself. It could mean someone born in the year of the Pig, or a person
coming from the Northwest direction (since Pig is in the Northwest
sector of the Luo Shu). In short, you need to use your own judgment in
deriving meaningful interpretation.
To observe these occurrences of evidence, you need to travel in the
direction as indicated by the special formation. For example, a “Yi Noble
Meeting Auspicious Door” formation may occur in the West sector of the
Qi Men Chart that you have selected.
This means, when you travel West (at the hour prescribed by that chart),
you will come across the occurrence of evidence as described in the
ancient text. And if you do see any signs of these occurrences, they
serve only to tell you that the special Qi Men structure is now active.
And shortly after, the outcome (positive or negative) as prescribed by
the special formation can be expected.
And for most of this section, you are required to know the difference
between the Host and the Guest. This is because each chart can be
good or bad, depending on which side are you on. One is proactive and
the other is responsive. Are you the Guest or are you the Host?
